<date>1529725231087</date><text>Pretty isolated unless you're already driving on the 14... Ordered fish and chips, got three pieces of fish on a pile of fries that were seasoned with seasoning salt, the fish was commercially breaded about 3 inches long with a very smooth looking batter, the ranch tasted as if it was from a store bought bottle, ordered lemon on the side, the tartar sauce was good, had iced tea with lemon.. $15 or something like that... Lots of history on the walls, a hole in the wall like setup showcasing the uniqueness of the restaurant, nice view of Ridgecrest and the valley... Family had various other items including filet mignon, chicken, baked potatoes etc.. two steak dinner for my brother and his wife was almost $70 with a side salad and baked potato. The house salad dressing is a blue cheese vinaigrette that's a little oily but good... Sounds gross but mix that house dressing with ranch and it's REALLY good. No sandwiches or wraps on the menu and unless it's steak it's pretty much deep fried.</text>< username>

<user>105929929840478959071</user><name>Jess Killips</name><Date>1380339301122< /Date>< rate>
4</rate>
< text>
I never thought much of Garcon because I've been to many of the highly acclaimed French restaurants in San Francisco, and didn't think a little place on the corner in the Mission would ever be able to compete. Plus, reviews were mixed and many people complained about the price. I was pleasantly surprised that Garcon delivered great food and even better cocktails. It was pricier than I expected, but it was good and I would definitely return for cocktails and appetizers!

* Complimentary Bread - Could not stop eating this.

* Black and Basil - 5 STARS: Black Pepper, Basil, lime, Vodka, and Gin. Wow, amazing cocktails. The cocktails here are serious contenders to my other Mission favorites, including Locanda, Range, Hog and Rocks, and Lolinda.

* Wine: Tuesdays = no corkage. Keep in mind you can't stack a 30% off Savored Discount on top of this deal. Thought the wines were pricey and overrated.

* Duck Liver Pate - 3.5 STARS: Very tasty pate, but not mind blowing.

* Mussels - 4 STARS: Fennel, shallot, lavender, lemon, pastis-chardonnay broth. I wanted to drink the broth. So light and tasty, and perfectly complemented with the bread.

* Duck - 4 STARS: Duck confit, twice cooked potatoes, frisee, arugula,  sunflower seed, vermouth vinaigrette. Amazing flavor, so delicious.

* Steak Frites - 4 STARS: Would have been a solid 5 stars except it was a little chewy, and I wasn't a huge fan of the short overly oily fries. The execution and sauces were incredible though!

* Creme Brulee - 4.5 STARS: Blood orange supremes, citrus vanilla syrup, lavender madeleine/ Everyone raves about this more than they should, but don't get me wrong, it was really good! Super creamy and rich but light at the same time. Not one of those super thick and chunky creme brulees.

* Panna Cotta - 1 STAR: Topped with melons. Very gelatinous and bouncy panna cotta, and the topping tasted a bit medicinal. Not my favorite dish of the night.<//text>

< Text>
My family had a GREAT time completing Jurassic Island and Awakening. Both created fun, cohesive stories with puzzles that were unique, challenging and doable.

If you have never done an escape room, I would recommend starting with Jurassic Island. There are a few surprises that kept the group entertained and  on our toes.

The Awakening is not "super scary" but that doesn't mean it wasn't good. We had two teens and two eleven year olds with us. They were pretty nervous but they found it was a "doable scary." They loved the creepiness, large rooms, and twists and turns at every corner.

The place was clean and the staff were very friendly. I also loved that it was private rooms - that really was great for our team. We completed both rooms. We used 1 hint in Jurassic Island and 4 in Awakening. We LOVED them and would 150% recommend for families, couples and friends.</Text>

<Review>We booked for Jurassic Island at 11pm. We arrived 20 minutes early and were asked if we wanted to start early as the game master had 2 rooms going at the same time. It was no problem to us so we started early. The room was good, wish the game master would have been more enthusiastic about the story to sell it more. So unfortunately, we didnt make it out of the room in the hour. My group and I have done almost all of the rooms (except private eye) and we've gotten out of all the rooms except this room. In the end the game master came in and was very pushy about getting us to leave. Normally the other game masters would have walked us through the rest of the game to show us the end result but he definitely let us know that it was a huge inconvenience to him. At first he told us he had to hurry up and reset the room because he had another group after us. When questioned about having another room at midnight he said oh yea sorry we are closed and I dont get paid after 12. We ended earlier than 12 and it would have taken him less than 3 minutes to explain the rest of the room to us. We have always been very satisfied with chronos however, this experience was very bad. <rate>5<//rate>< Text>
The rumor is true. This place is dope dope! I wish I could give this place 6 stars out of 5.

We have done couple espcae rooms before, but this was the best escape room I've done!

We did inception game The room itself was super fun and the puzzles were challenging enough but nothing too crazy that we could not figure out. There were a couple of moments where we got stuck but when we asked for a clue, it nudged us in the right direction. The room itself was set up extremely well and all the clues and puzzles were well thought out. It was a great experience in there. We all manage to work together and escaped the room with 12 minutes to spare!!! Apparently the record for this room is that a group managed to escape with 30+ minutes to spare (which is insane in our opinion, but apparently they have done over 100 escape the rooms). The stuff was super helpful and he explained the one of the puzzles to us since we accidentally managed to set it off and didn't actually solve it LOL

BE PREPARED TO THINK but don't overthink.< /Text>
